			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_1  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>With 27 years of experience in the North zone (Yishun). Kidsville Child Care &amp; Development Centre is a Voluntary Welfare Organisation&nbsp;is guided by theories founded by Jean Piaget and Lev Vygotsky which provides the base for a developmentally appropriate programme. It fosters active learning within an integrated curriculum.</p>
<p>Children across all levels engage in exploration based on a thematic approach.</p>
<p>We aim to promote a holistic development of children encompassing all areas of learning.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>

				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_9  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_dark">
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h2>Our</h2>
<h2>Philosophy</h2></div>
			</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_2 et_pb_column_15  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_10  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_dark">
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>To provide and maintain a comfortable, secure environment for children to develop physically, intellectually, socially and emotionally within an interactive and friendly atmosphere.</p>
<p>We believe that our team of trained and dedicated staff will provide the children with the enriching experiences needed to nurture and challenge their growing minds.</p>
<p>We believe in building a strong partnership with parents and the community to enhance the children’s holistic development.</p>
<p>We are certain that we can walk together in their learning journey.&nbsp;</p></div>
			</div>

				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>The parents are partners in their children’s learning journey. They are involved in the classrooms, outings, celebrations and partake in workshops organised by Kidsville and external bodies.</p></div>
